      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_701_and_800">
        List of lunar eclipses between 701 and 800
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_8th-century_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between 701 and 800">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There were 240 lunar eclipse events between 701 and 800 CE
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
